# ActivityLog

Use ActivityLog resource to request log information for completed jobs from the Monitor service. You can also request error logs and session logs. To request log information for jobs that are running, use the ActivityMonitor resource.

## Function: getAllActivityLog()

getAllAcitivityLog() returns all the activity logs from IICS in dict format.

>        Returns:
>            List of dict: <Activity Log in dict Format>

### Example:


```python
import infapy

# create infa handler
infaHandler = infapy.connect(profile="spani")
v2=infaHandler.v2()

# Perform getAllActivityLog()
ActivityLog=v2.getActivityLog()
print(ActivityLog.getAllActivityLog())
```

## Function: getActivityLogById()

getActivityLogById() returns activity logs as specified by the log id provided in the arguments.

>        Args:
>            id (string): ID of Log Entry.
>
>        Returns:
>            dict: <Activity Log in dict Format>

### Example:


```python
import infapy

# create infa handler
infaHandler = infapy.connect(profile="spani")
v2=infaHandler.v2()

# Perform getActivityLogById()
ActivityLog=v2.getActivityLog()
print(ActivityLog.getActivityLogById("0119Y4C1000000000QEH"))
```

    {'@type': 'activityLogEntry', 'id': '0119Y4C1000000000QEH', 'type': 'MTT', 'objectId': '0119Y40Z00000000001S', 'objectName': 'MT_Warning', 'runId': 6, 'startTime': '2021-09-23T03:01:16.000Z', 'endTime': '2021-09-23T03:01:46.000Z', 'startTimeUtc': '2021-09-23T07:01:16.000Z', 'endTimeUtc': '2021-09-23T07:01:46.000Z', 'state': 2, 'failedSourceRows': 0, 'successSourceRows': 4, 'failedTargetRows': 4, 'successTargetRows': 0, 'startedBy': 'admin021651', 'runContextType': 'ICS_UI', 'orgId': '0119Y4', 'totalSuccessRows': 0, 'totalFailedRows': 4, 'stopOnError': False, 'hasStopOnErrorRecord': True, 'items': [{'@type': 'activityLogEntryItem', 'id': '2752250614', 'type': 'MTT', 'objectId': '0119Y40Z00000000001S', 'objectName': '', 'runId': 6, 'agentId': '0119Y40800000000000A', 'runtimeEnvironmentId': '0119Y425000000000003', 'startTime': '2021-09-23T03:01:16.000Z', 'endTime': '2021-09-23T03:01:46.000Z', 'state': 2, 'errorMsg': 'WRT_8229 Database errors occurred: \nFnName: Execute -- [Informatica][ODBC Oracle Wire Protocol driver][Oracle]ORA-00001: unique constraint (SPANIA.MULTIPK_PK) violated', 'logEntryItemAttrs': {'CONSUMED_COMPUTE_UNITS': '0.0', 'ERROR_CODE': '8229', 'IS_SERVER_LESS': 'false', 'REQUESTED_COMPUTE_UNITS': '0.0', 'Session Log File Name': 's_mtt_8aA3LJ2OM7fkgCNryvrpCf_6.log'}, 'startedBy': 'admin021651', 'runContextType': 'ICS_UI', 'children': [], 'transformationEntries': [{'@type': 'transformationLogEntry', 'id': '5560747582', 'txName': 'Source', 'txType': 'SOURCE', 'successRows': 4, 'failedRows': 0}, {'@type': 'transformationLogEntry', 'id': '5560747585', 'txName': 'MULTIPK', 'txType': 'TARGET', 'successRows': 0, 'failedRows': 4}], 'sequenceValues': [], 'inOutParameterValues': []}]}
    

## Function: getActivityLogWithParams()

getActivityLogWithParams() returns activity logs as specified by the optional query parameters provided in the arguments.
If no query parameters are passed, it gives same result as getAllAcitivityLog().

>        Args:
>            offset (string, optional):  Number of rows to skip. Defaults to None.
>            rowLimit (string, optional):  Maximum number of rows to display. Defaults to None.
>            taskId (string, optional):  Task Id. Shows all activity logs for a particular task (subject to 
>                                        other parameters). Defaults to None.
>            runId (string, optional): Run Id. Shows all activity logs for a particular run Id across all 
>                                      tasks(subject to other parameters). Defaults to None.
>
>        Returns:
>            List of dict: <Activity Log in dict Format>

### Example:


```python
import infapy

# create infa handler
infaHandler = infapy.connect(profile="spani")
v2=infaHandler.v2()

# Perform getActivityLogWithParams()
ActivityLog=v2.getActivityLog()
print(ActivityLog.getActivityLogWithParams("2","2"))
```

## Function: getErrorLog()

getErrorLog() returns error logs as specified by the log id provided in the arguments. Writes error log to specified location with the specified filename, or default filename obtained from response.

>        Args:
>            id (string): ID of Log Entry.
>            location (string): Location of error log to be written. Special characters such as backslashes 
>                               must be escaped.
>            fileName (string, optional): Custom File Name of the error log. Defaults to None.
>
>        Returns:
>            String: <Download location of error log>

### Example 1: download error log with default file name


```python
import infapy

# create infa handler
infaHandler = infapy.connect(profile="spani")
v2=infaHandler.v2()

# Perform getErrorLog()
ActivityLog=v2.getActivityLog()
print(ActivityLog.getErrorLog("0119Y4C1000000000QPJ","C:\\Users\\spani\\Downloads"))
```

    Error Log download complete. Download Location: C:/Users/spani/Downloads/s_mtt_0119Y40Z00000000001S_8_error.csv
    

### Example 2: download error log with custom file name


```python
import infapy

# create infa handler
infaHandler = infapy.connect(profile="spani")
v2=infaHandler.v2()

# Perform getErrorLog()
ActivityLog=v2.getActivityLog()
print(ActivityLog.getErrorLog("0119Y4C1000000000QPJ","C:\\Users\\spani\\Downloads","try_Error.csv"))
```

    Error Log download complete. Download Location: C:/Users/spani/Downloads/try_Error.csv
    

## Function: getSessionLog()

getSessionLog() returns session logs for Data Integration Tasks and Linear Taskflows as specified by the log id provided in the arguments, and optional parameters.Writes session log to specified location with the specified filename, or default filename obtained from response.

>        Args:
>            id (string): ID of Log Entry.
>            location (string): Location of session log to be written. Special characters such as backslashes 
>                               must be escaped.
>            fileNameWithoutExt (string, optional): Custom File Name of the session log without extension. 
>                                                   Defaults to None.
>            itemId (string, optional): Item ID for subtask. Defaults to None.
>            childItemId (string, optional): Item ID for sub-subtask. Defaults to None.
>
>        Returns:
>            String: <Download location of error log>

### Example 1: download session log with default file name


```python
import infapy

# create infa handler
infaHandler = infapy.connect(profile="spani")
v2=infaHandler.v2()

# Perform getSessionLog()
ActivityLog=v2.getActivityLog()
print(ActivityLog.getSessionLog("0119Y4C1000000000QPJ","C:\\Users\\spani\\Downloads"))
```

    Session Log download complete. Download Location: C:/Users/spani/Downloads/log.log
    

### Example 2: download error log with custom file name


```python
import infapy

# create infa handler
infaHandler = infapy.connect(profile="spani")
v2=infaHandler.v2()

# Perform getSessionLog()
ActivityLog=v2.getActivityLog()
print(ActivityLog.getSessionLog("0119Y4C1000000000QPJ","C:\\Users\\spani\\Downloads","s_mtt_0119Y40Z00000000001S"))
```

    Session Log download complete. Download Location: C:/Users/spani/Downloads/s_mtt_0119Y40Z00000000001S.log
    

### Example 3: download session log for subtask


```python
import infapy

# create infa handler
infaHandler = infapy.connect(profile="spani")
v2=infaHandler.v2()

# Perform getSessionLog()
ActivityLog=v2.getActivityLog()
print(ActivityLog.getSessionLog("0119Y4C1000000000QPK","C:\\Users\\spani\\Downloads",itemId="2752306096",childItemId="2752306099"))
```

    Session Log download complete. Download Location: C:/Users/spani/Downloads/log.log
